this.budget_prevu - sum(this.depenses)` â‚¬\n> - **Progression** : `= round((sum(this.depenses) / this.budget_prevu) * 100, 1)`%\n\n## ðŸ“Š Indicateurs clÃ©s\n```dataviewjs\nconst tickets = dv.pages('\"10-COMPTA/Tickets\"')\n    .where(t => t.date >= \"2025-10-01\" && t.date <= \"2025-10-31\");\n\nconst total = tickets.array()\n    .reduce((sum, t) => sum + (t.montant_total || 0), 0);\n\nconst budget = 800;\nconst restant = budget - total;\nconst taux = (total / budget * 100).toFixed(1);\n\n// Barre de progression\nconst progression = \"â–ˆ\".repeat(Math.floor(taux/5)) + \"â–‘\".repeat(20 - Math.floor(taux/5));\n\ndv.paragraph(`**DÃ©pensÃ©** : ${total.toFixed(2)} â‚¬ / ${budget} â‚¬`);\ndv.paragraph(`[${progression}] ${taux}%`);\ndv.paragraph(``);\n\n// Statut\nif (taux < 50) {\n    dv.paragraph(`ðŸŸ¢ **Excellent !** Il reste ${restant.toFixed(2)}â‚¬`);\n} else if (taux < 80) {\n    dv.paragraph(`ðŸŸ¡ **Attention** : ${restant.toFixed(2)}â‚¬ restants`);\n} else if (taux < 100) {\n    dv.paragraph(`ðŸŸ  **Vigilance** : Seulement ${restant.toFixed(2)}â‚¬ restants`);\n} else {\n    dv.paragraph(`ðŸ”´ **ALERTE** : DÃ©passement de ${Math.abs(restant).toFixed(2)}â‚¬`);\n}\n```\n\n## ðŸ“… Tous les tickets du mois\n```dataview\nTABLE WITHOUT ID\n  file.link as \"Date\",\n  enseigne as \"Enseigne\",\n  montant_total as \"Montant\",\n  length(articles) as \"Articles\"\nFROM \"10-COMPTA/Tickets\"\nWHERE date >= date(\"2025-10-01\") AND date <= date(\"2025-10-31\")\nSORT date DESC\n```\n\n## ðŸ“ˆ RÃ©partition par catÃ©gorie\n```dataview\nTABLE WITHOUT ID\n  categorie as \"CatÃ©gorie\",\n  sum(rows.montant) as \"Total\",\n  round((sum(rows.montant) / 800) * 100, 1) + \"%\" as \"% Budget\"\nFROM \"10-COMPTA/Tickets\"\nWHERE date >= date(\"2025-10-01\") AND date <= date(\"2025-10-31\")\nFLATTEN categories as categorie\nGROUP BY categorie\nSORT sum(rows.montant) DESC\n```\n\n### Graphique\n```chart\ntype: pie\nlabels: [Alimentaire, Non-Alimentaire, Carburant, Restauration]\nseries:\n  - title: DÃ©penses\n    data: [348.50, 192.20, 48.64, 12.50]\nwidth: 80%\nlabelColors: true\n```\n\n## ðŸª RÃ©partition par enseigne\n```dataview\nTABLE WITHOUT ID\n  enseigne as \"Enseigne\",\n  count(rows) as \"Nb Tickets\",\n  sum(rows.montant_total) as \"Total â‚¬\"\nFROM \"10-COMPTA/Tickets\"\nWHERE date >= date(\"2025-10-01\") AND date <= date(\"2025-10-31\")\nGROUP BY enseigne\nSORT sum(rows.montant_total) DESC\n```\n\n## ðŸ“Š Analyse hebdomadaire\n\n| Semaine | dv.paragraph(`ðŸŸ¢ Dans les clous ! Dave Ramsey\n\n## ðŸŽ¯ Vue d'ensemble\n\n### ðŸ“Š Indicateurs Mois en Cours\n```dataviewjs\nconst maintenant = new Date();\nconst annee = maintenant.getFullYear();\nconst mois = String(maintenant.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');\nconst premierJour = `${annee}-${mois}-01`;\nconst dernierJour = new Date(annee, maintenant.getMonth() + 1, 0);\nconst dernierJourStr = `${annee}-${mois}-${String(dernierJour.getDate()).padStart(2, '0')}`;\n\nconst tickets = dv.pages('\"10-COMPTA/Tickets\"')\n    .where(t => t.date >= premierJour && t.date <= dernierJourStr);\n\nconst total = tickets.array().reduce((sum, t) => sum + (t.montant_total || 0), 0);\nconst budget = 800;\nconst restant = budget - total;\nconst nbTickets = tickets.length;\nconst panierMoyen = nbTickets > 0 ? total / nbTickets : 0;\n\n// Affichage sous forme de cards\ndv.header(3, \"ðŸ’° Budget\");\ndv.paragraph(`**${total.toFixed(2)} â‚¬** / ${budget} â‚¬`);\nconst pct = Math.round((total/budget)*100);\nconst bars = \"â–ˆ\".repeat(Math.floor(pct/5)) + \"â–‘\".repeat(20-Math.floor(pct/5));\ndv.paragraph(`[${bars}] ${pct}%`);\n\ndv.header(3, \"ðŸŽ« Tickets\");\ndv.paragraph(`**${nbTickets}** tickets ce mois`);\ndv.paragraph(`Panier moyen : **${panierMoyen.toFixed(2)} â‚¬**`);\n\ndv.header(3, \"ðŸ“ˆ Tendance\");\nif (pct < 50) dv.paragraph(\"ðŸŸ¢ Excellent\");\nelse if (pct < 80) dv.paragraph(\"ðŸŸ¡ Vigilance\");\nelse if (pct < 100) dv.paragraph(\"ðŸŸ  Attention\");\nelse dv.paragraph(\"ðŸ”´ DÃ©passement\");\n```\n\n---\n\n## ðŸ“¥ Ã€ Traiter (Inbox)\n```dataview\nTABLE WITHOUT ID\n  file.link as \"Ticket\",\n  date as \"Date\",\n  montant_total as \"Montant\"\nFROM \"00-INBOX\"\nWHERE contains(tags, \"compta/a-traiter\")\nSORT date DESC\n```\n\n---\n\n## ðŸ• ActivitÃ© RÃ©cente\n\n### Derniers tickets (7 jours)\n```dataview\nTABLE WITHOUT ID\n  file.link as \"Date\",\n  enseigne as \"Enseigne\",\n  montant_total as \"Montant\",\n  choice(contains(tags, \"promo\"), \"ðŸ·ï¸\", \"\") as \"Promo\"\nFROM \"10-COMPTA/Tickets\"\nWHERE date >= date(today) - dur(7 days)\nSORT date DESC\nLIMIT 10\n```\n\n---\n\n## ðŸ† Top 5 du Mois\n\n### ðŸª Enseignes\n```dataview\nTABLE WITHOUT ID\n  enseigne as \"Enseigne\",\n  count(rows) as \"Tickets\",\n  sum(rows.montant_total) as \"Total\"\nFROM \"10-COMPTA/Tickets\"\nWHERE date >= date(today) - dur(30 days)\nGROUP BY enseigne\nSORT sum(rows.montant_total) DESC\nLIMIT 5\n```\n\n### ðŸ›’ Produits\n```dataview\nTABLE WITHOUT ID\n  produit as \"Produit\",\n  count(rows) as \"Achats\",\n  sum(rows.montant) as \"Total\"\nFROM \"10-COMPTA/Tickets\"\nWHERE date >= date(today) - Dataview Queries AvancÃ©es\n1. Produits jamais achetÃ©s depuis X jours\ndataviewTABLE WITHOUT ID\n  file.link as \"Produit\",\n  derniere_achat as \"Dernier achat\",\n  round((date(today) - derniere_achat).days, 0) as \"Jours Ã©coulÃ©s\"\nFROM \"10-COMPTA/Produits\"\nWHERE derniere_achat < date(today) - dur(30 days)\nSORT derniere_achat ASC\n2. Dave Ramsey\n\n## ðŸŽ¯ Vue d'ensemble\n\n### ðŸ“Š Indicateurs Mois en Cours\n```dataviewjs\nconst maintenant = new Date();\nconst annee = maintenant.getFullYear();\nconst mois = String(maintenant.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');\nconst premierJour = `${annee}-${mois}-01`;\nconst dernierJour = new Date(annee, maintenant.getMonth() + 1, 0);\nconst dernierJourStr = `${annee}-${mois}-${String(dernierJour.getDate()).padStart(2, '0')}`;\n\nconst tickets = dv.pages('\"10-COMPTA/Tickets\"')\n    .where(t => t.date >= premierJour && t.date <= dernierJourStr);\n\nconst total = tickets.array().reduce((sum, t) => sum + (t.montant_total || 0), 0);\nconst budget = 800;\nconst restant = budget - total;\nconst nbTickets = tickets.length;\nconst panierMoyen = nbTickets > 0 ? total / nbTickets : 0;\n\n// Affichage sous forme de cards\ndv.header(3, \"ðŸ’° Budget\");\ndv.paragraph(`**${total.toFixed(2)} â‚¬** / ${budget} â‚¬`);\nconst pct = Math.round((total/budget)*100);\nconst bars = \"â–ˆ\".repeat(Math.floor(pct/5)) + \"â–‘\".repeat(20-Math.floor(pct/5));\ndv.paragraph(`[${bars}] ${pct}%`);\n\ndv.header(3, \"ðŸŽ« Tickets\");\ndv.paragraph(`**${nbTickets}** tickets ce mois`);\ndv.paragraph(`Panier moyen : **${panierMoyen.toFixed(2)} â‚¬**`);\n\ndv.header(3, \"ðŸ“ˆ Tendance\");\nif (pct < 50) dv.paragraph(\"ðŸŸ¢ Excellent\");\nelse if (pct < 80) dv.paragraph(\"ðŸŸ¡ Vigilance\");\nelse if (pct < 100) dv.paragraph(\"ðŸŸ  Attention\");\nelse dv.paragraph(\"ðŸ”´ DÃ©passement\");\n```\n\n---\n\n## ðŸ“¥ Ã€ Traiter (Inbox)\n```dataview\nTABLE WITHOUT ID\n  file.link as \"Ticket\",\n  date as \"Date\",\n  montant_total as \"Montant\"\nFROM \"00-INBOX\"\nWHERE contains(tags, \"compta/a-traiter\")\nSORT date DESC\n```\n\n---\n\n## ðŸ• ActivitÃ© RÃ©cente\n\n### Derniers tickets (7 jours)\n```dataview\nTABLE WITHOUT ID\n  file.link as \"Date\",\n  enseigne as \"Enseigne\",\n  montant_total as \"Montant\",\n  choice(contains(tags, \"promo\"), \"ðŸ·ï¸\", \"\") as \"Promo\"\nFROM \"10-COMPTA/Tickets\"\nWHERE date >= date(today) - dur(30 days)\nGROUP BY enseigne\nSORT sum(rows.montant_total) DESC\nLIMIT 5\n```\n\n### ðŸ›’ Produits\n```dataview\nTABLE WITHOUT ID\n  produit as \"Produit\",\n  count(rows) as \"Achats\",\n  sum(rows.montant) as \"Total\"\nFROM \"10-COMPTA/Tickets\"\nWHERE date >= date(today) - total;\nconst nbTickets = tickets.length;\nconst panierMoyen = nbTickets > 0 ? total / nbTickets : 0;\n\n// Affichage sous forme de cards\ndv.header(3, \"ðŸ’° Budget\");\ndv.paragraph(`**${total.toFixed(2)} â‚¬** / ${budget} â‚¬`);\nconst pct = Math.round((total/budget)*100);\nconst bars = \"â–ˆ\".repeat(Math.floor(pct/5)) + \"â–‘\".repeat(20-Math.floor(pct/5));\ndv.paragraph(`[${bars}] ${pct}%`);\n\ndv.header(3, \"ðŸŽ« Tickets\");\ndv.paragraph(`**${nbTickets}** tickets ce mois`);\ndv.paragraph(`Panier moyen : **${panierMoyen.toFixed(2)} â‚¬**`);\n\ndv.header(3, \"ðŸ“ˆ Tendance\");\nif (pct < 50) dv.paragraph(\"ðŸŸ¢ Excellent\");\nelse if (pct < 80) dv.paragraph(\"ðŸŸ¡ Vigilance\");\nelse if (pct < 100) dv.paragraph(\"ðŸŸ  Attention\");\nelse dv.paragraph(\"ðŸ”´ DÃ©passement\");\n```\n\n---\n\n## ðŸ“¥ Ã€ Traiter (Inbox)\n```dataview\nTABLE WITHOUT ID\n  file.link as \"Ticket\",\n  date as \"Date\",\n  montant_total as \"Montant\"\nFROM \"00-INBOX\"\nWHERE contains(tags, \"compta/a-traiter\")\nSORT date DESC\n```\n\n---\n\n## ðŸ• ActivitÃ© RÃ©cente\n\n### Derniers tickets (7 jours)\n```dataview\nTABLE WITHOUT ID\n  file.link as \"Date\",\n  enseigne as \"Enseigne\",\n  montant_total as \"Montant\",\n  choice(contains(tags, \"promo\"), \"ðŸ·ï¸\", \"\") as \"Promo\"\nFROM \"10-COMPTA/Tickets\"\nWHERE date >= date(today) - dur(30 days)\nGROUP BY enseigne\nSORT sum(rows.montant_total) DESC\nLIMIT 5\n```\n\n### ðŸ›’ Produits\n```dataview\nTABLE WITHOUT ID\n  produit as \"Produit\",\n  count(rows) as \"Achats\",\n  sum(rows.montant) as \"Total\"\nFROM \"10-COMPTA/Tickets\"\nWHERE date >= date(today) -
